16a4(15): rgyal ba chan de ba'i yengs 'dzin chen me bstan 'dzin rnam dag don po che'i phyag ds/ khri brtan ned bu rcsi'i ds mdzed chang nas deb gzugs su dse bgrigs gnang ba'i dba phreng rapa ma dse gtsod bzhag byas 
16a5(15): theg/ sde dgongs zhig dgen pa'i lha sde mgad da tshang gi dos rnying lag bris yig nag can dang 'dra bsnud byas te/ mngon gsal can gyi chad lhag dang rkyen cha then degs la cha brkangs byas pa las rtsa ba'i ma dpe'i 
16a6(15): gzhung 'gres la/ bsdud dpes bces brgyud ma byas pa sed bzhag byas yo// go dam bsgrigs sangs dang yang rung gi khyad par ma 'dra ba'i dse rgyun du ma yed na'ang / 'did ma ds ji nad ser bzhag byas te bged bgrigs / 
16b1(15): byas yo// / e snang dogs pa zhig ste/ mgad da tshang gi lag bris yig nag ds rnying can dang // bal khyung dgen pa'i bka' 'gyud gras su yed pa'i 'phrul dpad can segs la yi khri mtha' sel dang 'brel yid kyi dpe ma / 
16b2(15): / 
16b3(15): ma 'dra ba bka' brnten gyi rnam par gnas bze can du mad 'dug pa rnams/ d/ lan dpo tshegs 'did ma 'das na'ang / rjes su de'i thad gzigs mtshan rnam pas de lugs kyis de snang mdzad gal ce ba'i bsgrul ma dang / 
16b4(15): bcas ti gi bazni mdzad lnga'i dp rnying phyegs bgrigs / kyo ad grangs rabpar zhas bgrigs byas yed kyang ddung ma rtegs dbang gis cad lhagsegs yod nges te/ spyi la bbyad sngen lo nga lnga brgya lhag 
16b5(15): nas gangs can nad kyi yul du yi ga' par khang 'jzugs bskun dang // se gzhi legs bsgrigs byas pa'i 'grems spel yengs khyab byed srel dad zin na'ang / g.yung dung bean gyi dse gzhi' bsdu bsgrigs byed pa'o ga skabs / 
16b6(15): kyi thad sug de tsam byung med pas/ 'did phyegs la nyams myeng dang lag len segs la mig nes len gzhi dken pas gam cha gsar du yin pa dang / ges su de zhus bgrigs pa che yang mkhyen dpyed dab 'byams pa / 
16b7(15): yin chad/ 'di' thad mthun rkyen zung la 'gal rkyen lang ba'i gseb ru dal brling 'grig pa dang ma byung na/ phyegs gang so'i thed yug dang gnas sangs tshad las brgal ba'i legs ma zhig then thabs med pas// 
17a1(15): by/ lags kyis rjes su gzigs mthan nas kho hUM i i tshi/ pas 'di la dog kyen cad ye brang yong nges gnang de che ning / 
17a2(15): 'di ye byas pa 'das kyang sad du gsung dung ban gyi lung gi bstan rjing rd h hsorjopa don po che gsal dag 'grog po' nabs tshu' grabs 
17a3(15): bsdegs tsham du 'gyud rnam che ba bcas/ 'byung ldan o myd d / cobdab byung shing rha lo'i zla ches rarnyen/ 
17a4(15): smyo la rabnyin/ byung po nang chen dgen yrh/ rgo mdz dpe thus tshan pas//
